Oil Market: Substantial Volume of Asphalt for Soap Making 255

Asphalt is typically slow-moving during the summer, as candle makers cease production during hot weather, leaving only the soap-making industry as a consumer. In the last decade, numerous soap factories have sprung up in Shanghai, resulting in significant asphalt consumption. However, in the past three to four years, several major factories have been selling soap at exceptionally low prices, aiming to eliminate smaller factories. This has had a severe impact, with some smaller factories unable to survive and ceasing operations, while others have significantly reduced production. Local asphalt merchants previously enjoyed a steady stream of small orders from these factories from spring to summer, but this has now consolidated into larger transactions. Major soap factories typically purchase in bulk, making it difficult for smaller oil merchants to compete. Moreover, large-volume transactions offer very thin profit margins, leading some to withdraw from the market. Consequently, asphalt merchants are less enthusiastic about stocking up for the summer compared to previous years. Since two years ago, a grocery store in Nanshi has also started trading asphalt, specializing in sales to soap factories. Their annual volume is reportedly over 30,000 dan, far exceeding the capacity of dedicated asphalt merchants. Last week saw 2,000-3,000 dan traded at prices slightly above 20 taels, all from this grocery store. They source directly from Yichang and Shashi, bypassing merchants in Hankou, allowing them to offer lower prices. As a result, asphalt merchants have been forced to retreat. Current total inventory in Shanghai is estimated at 2,000-3,000 pieces. The market is extremely sluggish due to the lack of small orders from soap factories and the cessation of candle production. Activity is expected to resume after the Mid-Autumn Festival when candle production restarts. Recent reports from Hankou indicate extremely low inventory levels and strong demand. Sourcing has been halted for a long time due to hot weather preventing transportation. Macheng oil is priced at 16.2 taels, Jingmen oil is priced at 16.4 taels, Zhijiang oil is priced at 16.2 taels, Pingjing oil has no market, estimated at 15.6-15.8 taels, and Jinshi oil is priced slightly above 15 taels. Local oil prices are set, but there are no transactions, resulting in a very quiet market.

North-South Goods: New Hainan Dried Longan Expected to Fall 256

Land Prices Ease. New Hainan dried longan was previously offered at 40 taels. Reports indicate that North-South merchants have received another 100+ pieces, and land prices are reportedly easing. The opening price for this batch is expected to decline. The opening price should be announced today, with further details to follow.

Comments

Throwing Away the Official Cap 257

— Fo

Wang Jingwei, because Zhang Xueliang possessed a large army, but lost the land of three provinces within a few days, and did not resist, and later Jinzhou was captured, also watching without helping. Now that Rehe is in danger, Beijing and Tianjin are shaken, the Central Government ordered Zhang to send troops to resist the violent Japanese and recover the lost territory. But Zhang made many threats and refused to send troops, so Wang threw away his official cap, vowing not to cooperate with Zhang. Zhang Xueliang saw that Wang Jingwei had already thrown away his official cap, and had no face to linger in his position. Although he did not sincerely want to resign, he could not help but throw away his official cap on the surface, and also asked to resign. However, he also said that the Premier of the Executive Yuan could leave immediately after throwing away his cap, but I, the commander of the army, cannot leave immediately after throwing it away, and must have an explanation. Therefore, although Zhang Xueliang did not sincerely resign, he did throw away his official cap to some extent. The ministers of various departments, because of Wang's resignation this time, were determined, and there was no room for retention. Therefore, the ministers of various departments of the Central Government, as the leaders of the responsible cabinet, had firmly resigned. In order to express their intention to advance and retreat together, they also threw away their official caps together. Although this kind of cap throwing was intended to persuade Wang to stay, it still counts as throwing away the official cap.

When Jiang Jieshi heard that Wang had thrown away his cap, he urgently telegraphed He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, etc., saying that Wang's resignation must be firmly retained no matter what. If Wang insists on not doing it, I will also resign. This means that Jiang is also willing to throw away his cap. However, Jiang's throwing away his cap is nothing more than expressing his determination to retain Wang, but it cannot be said that he is not making a gesture of throwing away his cap.

At a time when the international situation is very serious, it is truly unfortunate to throw away the official caps together, truly unfortunate. However, the main cause of this cap throwing is mostly due to Zhang Xueliang. If Zhang sincerely resigns, then many caps can be taken back. However, while Zhang expressed his resignation, he still expressed that his army must be commanded by someone. Whether he is sincerely throwing away his cap or pretending to throw it away, we can only wait and see what happens next.

In Memory of Mr. Ye Huijun 258

— Chen Ziyi

Mr. Chen's eight poems in memory of Mr. Ye Huijun, now excerpting four of them on the left:

How many generations in the region formed alliances,

I knew his name thirty years ago.

Suddenly, the wind and clouds spread through Shanghai,

Giving way to Mr. Ye for recording achievements is appropriate.

A hundred and eight mani beads bind this body,

Enjoying Zen in his later years was also a predestined cause.

His compassionate heart wanted to save the suffering people everywhere,

Half for the sorrow of heaven and half for the pity of man.

(Mr. Ye was devoted to Buddhism in his later years and became more enthusiastic about charitable causes.)

Discussing the future with like minds,

Considering and repeatedly deliberating on stabilizing grain prices.

His grand plan was originally not inferior at the time,

And we still follow his guidance today.

(At the beginning of the Shanghai Grain Exchange, Mr. Ye was engaged elsewhere. I moved him with the righteousness of fellow industry and unity, and then we planned together.)

Worry and joy, gain and loss for ten springs,

Sharing the same boat in wind and rain, we were even closer.

In recent years, I have been afraid of passing by the yellow mud wine shop,

Another predecessor has withered away.

New Methods of Scientific Leather Making 260

— Lü Ziwei

Leather has many uses, such as making leather shoes, leather bags, cloth belts, and wallets. These all use it as a raw material. This kind of leather must be soft, beautiful in color, strong, durable, resistant to water stains and sun exposure to be considered qualified. The raw material for leather is raw hide. The hides of various animals are the raw material. Then, potassium dichromate, alum, tannic acid, etc., are used to give it special effects, that is, it does not decay, does not harden, is durable, can waterproof, and is not afraid of sun exposure.

(1) Various methods of leather making The medicinal materials used for raw hides can be divided into three categories: (1) Animal oils are applied to the back of the raw hide and heated to gradually oxidize it into an oily leather. (2) Raw hides are soaked in vegetable tannic acid (i.e., bark) to become red leather. (3) Mineral substances are used to make leather. This method is divided into two categories: (A) Alum and salt are used to pickle the hide to make white leather. (B) Potassium dichromate or chrome alum is used to soak the raw hide to make a light green color, which is called chrome leather (commonly known as camel leather, which is a misnomer).

(2) Complete procedures for the new method of leather making (A) Preparation... Remove the dirt on the hide, make the hide swell, and make it easier to absorb the medicinal solution. (B) Tanning... Soak the hide in the medicinal solution to make it a strong leather. (C) Finishing... Tidy up and decorate it to make it beautiful and attract people to buy it.

(3) Preparation of leather making The preparation methods can be divided into six types: (1) soaking in water, (2) liming, (3) hair removal, (4) fleshing, (5) deliming, and (6) acid pickling. (1) Soaking in water is to: (A) remove unclean substances; (B) dissolve salt; make the hide easy to swell.

(2) Liming is to: (A) destroy the cells around the hair roots to make the hair fall off; (B) swell the hide surface to make it easier to absorb the medicinal solution; (C) remove the fat in the hide. The method is to soak the hide in lime water solution, stir it, and add some sodium sulfide. (3) Hair removal Use a dull knife to scrape off the hair. (4) Fleshing Scrape off the meat on the surface of the hide. (5) Deliming Wash off the lime water, the method is to soak bird droppings in water, take the clear solution on the surface, soak the hide in it, stir it frequently, take it out after about a week. (6) Acid pickling is to: (A) shrink the hide: (B) neutralize water and lime.

(4) Tanning and finishing There are two types of chrome tanning methods: (A) Use (A) (1) 5 pounds of potassium dichromate (2) 2.5 pounds of hydrochloric acid (3) 400 pounds of water (B) (1) 10 pounds of sodium thiosulfate (2) 5 pounds of hydrochloric acid (3) 40 gallons of water (based on 100 pounds of raw hide). First soak the hide in the two solutions of (A), take it out when it turns yellow, blow it for a day and night, and then put it into the solution of (B). (B) Use (1) Chrome alum 15 pounds, (2) Lead carbonate 4.5 pounds, (3) Salt 4.5 pounds, (4) Water 150 pounds (based on 100 pounds of raw hide). Put the swollen hide into it without stirring, the longer the better, so that the medicinal solution penetrates into the hide. After soaking the hide in the two solutions of (A) and (B), dye it to make it beautiful and shiny, and the leather making process is successful.

Society for Improving Social Customs Discussion

My Views on Improving the Kitchen 261

— Fearless

As Mr. Chi Fo said, the cleanliness of a kitchen is closely related to the health of a family. Therefore, the kitchen does need to be improved. Now I will write down my humble opinions and hope that the members will correct them.

1. The kitchen must be large In Shanghai, general capitalists/landlords only want to build more houses and collect more rent, so the openness of the houses has become narrower. The kitchen seems to be even more unnecessary in the eyes of the landlords, so it is as small as a dried tofu. However, in Shanghai, three or four households often live in a single Shikumen building. When cooking, they all gather in the kitchen. If there are too many people, it may not be easy to keep it clean? In the hot weather, three or four people are crowded in a small kitchen, and the heat and crowds are likely to cause epidemics. Also, because the houses are small, firewood and other kindling materials are piled in the kitchen. May I ask, in such a small kitchen, how can we be sure that there will be no danger? Therefore, I think the kitchen must be enlarged.

2. The kitchen equipment must be simple Since the kitchens in Shanghai are so small, as mentioned above, it will only be effective if the landlords are willing to show mercy and improve them. Otherwise, it is useless for us tenants to just talk about it on paper. Therefore, under the pressure of small kitchens, we can only make up for it by using simple equipment. The kitchen is already very unclean due to the oily fumes, and if we pile up unnecessary things, it will be even more chaotic and unclean. Therefore, I think that in addition to the necessary stove, the kitchen only needs a table for picking vegetables or cutting meat, etc. At most, we can put a bowl cabinet. As for rice straw and the like, it is best not to put them in the kitchen. Also, those who are slightly wealthy, it is best to whitewash the kitchen once a year, because the kitchen is the easiest place to hide dirt. Spiders and the like often weave webs in the kitchen. The above are just some temporary thoughts, and they are also the most superficial two points for improving the kitchen.

Re-Improving Dining 262

— Wen

Yesterday, I saw the publication in this journal of Mr. Yiyiguanzhu's suggestions for improving dining. After reading it, I have some doubts. Now I will state my humble opinions and hope that the wise will correct them.

What Mr. Yiyiguanzhu calls (communal eating) is that several people eat from the same bowl of vegetables or soup. After repeated dipping of everyone's chopsticks and spoons, this bowl of vegetables or soup will invisibly add a lot of saliva. If one of these people has tuberculosis or other infectious diseases, then his germs will inevitably spread from his chopsticks or spoon to the food. The other healthy people who eat this food contaminated with germs will be in danger.

The above is the meaning of Mr. Yiyiguanzhu. I think that in a family, since there are people with tuberculosis or other infectious diseases, in fact, the rest of the people should take extra precautions everywhere. Improving dining is not necessary, because the invisible spread of (germs) | in the air, on tables, chairs, utensils, etc. | not only in (communal eating), improving to (individual eating) can avoid everything. Moreover, this kind of communal eating has been passed down from ancient times to the present. Assuming that its danger is so great, then if it has been passed down to the present, modern China would probably have been difficult to exist.

As for (in recent years, Chinese people have been Europeanized in everything...), may I ask where is the Europeanization? Everything is still at the mercy of others and breathing the breath of others. What has been transformed is nothing more than public social interaction! Men and women dancing! All the romance! And what Mr. Yiyiguanzhu calls Europeanization, I don't know what it is? At the same time, I don't know whether Mr. Yiyiguanzhu also sympathizes with such Europeanization? (Reply)

Family Issues

A Family That Spoils Their Children 263

— Kang Shi

The old Ma couple next door are a pair of people who believe in spoiling their children, which has led to bad habits in their children. I will now write about it in detail below. The old couple has two sons and two daughters and runs a XX shop, and their livelihood is quite prosperous.

Their youngest son is almost twenty years old and has studied for many years, costing them several thousand dollars. However, he only knows how to wear Western suits, watch movies, and ask his parents for money, spending his days in laziness and idleness. His parents are believers in spoiling their children, so they let him squander his money. Sometimes, some relatives advise him to find a job, recommending him to a position in one or two companies, but, being accustomed to laziness and idleness, he naturally cannot devote himself to his duties, and the salary of thirty or forty dollars is not enough for him to squander for a few days, so after a few days, he is unwilling to continue working, returning home to enjoy comfort. This has happened many times.

He got married last spring, but he has no productivity, so of course all expenses are supplied by his parents. He has to change several sets of Western suits every day, which troubles the housemaid at home, who cannot keep up with washing the clothes.

The eldest daughter is also of marriageable age, and spends her days eating sweets and other snacks, especially liking to mingle with men, so her reputation is somewhat poor. However, her parents do not prohibit or control her. Like the family above, we can determine that they are corrupt, decadent, and also social parasites.

School Scene

A School Divided for Spoils 264

— Xian Zhang

I dropped out of school after graduating from junior high school, because the school I was attending at the time only had junior high school. To avoid mistakenly entering the countless "wild chicken" middle schools in Shanghai, I came up with a very pitiful and stupid method, which was to choose those famous schools with a long history. After carefully and meticulously reviewing the newspapers, I found that X Middle School was recruiting new students. I had long heard of X Middle School, and its name was like thunder in my ears.

In addition, I had a relative who was also studying there, so I resolutely went to take the entrance examination. Originally, I thought that the recruitment of the famous X Middle School must be very strict, and the exam questions must be very complex and difficult, but to my surprise, X Middle School's recruitment was not really an exam, and there were no exam questions. A recruiting teacher only asked where I had studied before, and also roughly asked about some book titles I had read in my previous school, collected a dollar for the registration fee, and looked at my diploma. The so-called entrance exam was over. He said very frankly, "You can come to pay the fees and start classes on XX month XX day." I walked out of X Middle School with a stomach full of doubts and surprise. Afterwards, I went to the home of a relative who was studying at X Middle School to find out the truth. According to his reply:

X Middle School was originally a very ordinary school, and the usual discipline was not very strict, and the students' grades were also very ordinary. After the January 28th Incident, X Middle School was indirectly affected by the war and became even worse. For some reason, other schools that were affected by the disaster all returned to their original state after the war, and students were pouring in and out of the stuffy, small classrooms in groups. However, X Middle School, probably because the students all lived in the war zone, only saw a sudden decrease in students and no increase. This made the school authorities very worried. With fewer students, the income from tuition fees naturally decreased, and with less tuition fees, the teachers' salaries naturally had to be reduced. Better teachers were naturally unwilling to hibernate here anymore and packed their bags and left voluntarily. Clumsy teachers, who originally regarded X Middle School as the only place to solve their livelihood problems, naturally could not leave, so they had to take on the heavy and important subjects concurrently. The clever and wise principal did not want to lose the achievements of hard work and the reputation in society over the years, so he came up with a very clever compromise: to avoid the teachers being resentful and complaining, and of course to avoid the school authorities losing money, which was to take the students' tuition fees, and after deducting a portion of the necessary school administrative expenses, the remainder was divided up like spoils: the principal taking X shares, the teachers X shares, and the school employees X shares. This fair method made the teachers very happy, so the bad habit of indiscriminately recruiting new students occurred, and you were also deceived by them." After hearing these words, I was silent, and at the same time I realized a great truth. China's territory is divided up into your piece and my piece, so naturally this phenomenon will also occur in schools. This is a natural thing, so what is there to be surprised about?

The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days. If the fine is not paid, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for two yuan. Opium paraphernalia and red pills, etc., are confiscated as listed. ▲ Hongkou Police Station v. Wang Lu et al. Opium Case (Main Text) Wang Lu is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 100 yuan for providing a place for others to smoke opium with the intention of profiting. He Guang and Wang Di are each given a reduced sentence of one month of imprisonment and fined 40 yuan for the crime of smoking opium. Zhu Zhou, a recidivist, is given a reduced sentence of one month of imprisonment for the attempted crime of smoking opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall each be used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days. If the fine is not paid, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for two yuan. The smoking paraphernalia, etc., are confiscated as listed. Li Ji is given a two-year suspension. ▲ Jiaxing Road Police Station v. Huang Bingcai Obstruction Case (Main Text) Huang Bingcai is given a reduced sentence of three months of imprisonment for the crime of injuring others by using a method sufficient to cause death. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days.

Criminal Judgments ▲ Police Department v. Liu Gendao Theft Case (Main Text) Liu Gendao is sentenced to 40 days of detention with a two-year suspension for theft. ▲ Police Department v. Qiao Caoshi is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of abducting a woman under the age of twenty from the person with parental rights. Cai Wushi is sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for the crime of abducting a woman under the age of twenty with the intention of profiting. ▲ Public Notice Public Notice Regarding Auction Matters This court is executing the case of creditor Tao Liangong v. debtor Xie Chunsheng regarding debt disputes. The court has sealed and appraised the debtor's property listed below. The auction is scheduled for August 19 at 8:00 AM. The court will dispatch a clerk to direct the bailiff to implement the auction with the assistance of the judicial police. Residents who wish to purchase the said property should report to the Bailiff's Office of this court to obtain a permit to inspect the property at its location and then participate in the auction on time. If there are two or more bidders, the bidder with the highest price will be the purchaser. The purchaser shall pay the full price on the spot, and the auctioned property will be given to him/her for collection. All residents are hereby notified. Special notice.
